11.1(1): gsum pa'o// //

235.2(1): rnams mtshon pa 'di lta ste/ e ma ho/ bon nyid rang bzhin rnam par dag /'dus

235.14(1): gang yang med/ 'dzin pa med par rang 'byung gi/ ngo bo nyid du rtogs pa'o/ /sgrub

235.17(1): bcos pa gang yang med/ bla na med pa'i 'bras bu nyid/ rang la rdzogs shing chub pa

272.3(1): skad snyan/ rag ta 'thung na lta mdog sdug /mang sa zos na mthu cher 'gyur/ byang 
272.4(1): sems zos na sku tshe ring / rigs lnga 'grub pa'i yon tan ni/ dri chen de bzhin 
272.5(1): gshegs pa'i rigs/ g.yung drung sems ni g.yung drung rigs/ dri chu las kyi rigs 
272.6(1): yin no/ /pad ma rag ta dbang gi rigs/ mang sa rin chen rigs yin no/ /sdug 
272.7(1): bsngal kun las grol 'gyur zhing / dngos grub rnam gnyis thabs pa'i phyir/ bsgrub

272.9(1): pa'i thabs kyis ni/ ma nor lus la bstan pa ni/ bdud rtsi lnga'i ril lu nyid/ byas 
272.10(1): ste snying shun nang du dril/ skra'i gseb du btags gyur na/ yon tan brjod las 
272.11(1): 'das par 'gyur/ yang na dar khug dril byas nas/ lus la 'chang nas dus skabs 
272.12(1): su/ bdud rtsi sman mchod byas gyur na/ de'i yon tan bsam mi khyab/ dang du blang

272.14(1): 'gu ya srog 'dzin g.yung drung gsang ba'i rgyud las/ dang du blang ba'i dam tshig 
272.15(1): bstan pa'i le'u ste bco lnga pa'o//

272.21(1): dang ni ye shes lnga/ rigs kyi yab lnga yum lnga dang / sku gsung thugs dang yon tan

273.2(1): lta ste/ rigs lnga yab lnga 'di lta ste/ de bzhin rigs dang g.yung drung rigs/ las

273.10(1): li mun lan brgyad dang / me'i tshangs stang dbal mo dang / chu'i ting nam gtum mo 
273.11(1): dang / sku lnga la'ang 'di lta ste/ ma bcos pa ni bon gyi sku/ zhing khams dag pa

458.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
458.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
458.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
458.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
458.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
458.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
458.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
458.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
458.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
458.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
458.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi 
458.20(1): ma 'gro kun yongs la shar ba'i smon 'dun dang bcas 'byung ldan 3 1 spyi lo 2 15 5[ / ]1
458.21(1): nyin/ g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang nas bris/ /
